module: srl_nokia-acl
  +--rw acl
     +--rw ipv4-filter* [name]
     |  +--rw name                     srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw description?             srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  +--rw subinterface-specific?   enumeration {not srl_nokia-feat:future-0-0}?
     |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?    boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:future-0-0}?
     |  +--ro last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |     +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |     +--ro tcam-entries
     |     |  +--ro forwarding-complex* [complex-identifier]
     |     |     +--ro complex-identifier    string
     |     |     +--ro single-instance?      uint16
     |     |     +--ro input-total?          uint16 {not srl_nokia-feat:future-0-0}?
     |     |     +--ro output-total?         uint16 {not srl_nokia-feat:future-0-0}?
     |     +--rw action
     |     |  +--rw (action)?
     |     |     +--:(accept)
     |     |     |  +--rw accept!
     |     |     |     +--rw rate-limit {srl_nokia-feat:subif-acl-policer,(not srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-h2) and (not srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-h3) and (not srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-h4)}?
     |     |     |        +--rw policer?   -> ../../../../../../policers/policer/name
     |     |     +--:(drop)
     |     |        +--rw drop!
     |     |           +--rw log?   boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:future-0-0}?
     |     +--rw match
     |     |  +--rw destination-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  +--rw dscp-set*           srl_nokia-comm:dscp {srl_nokia-feat:ip-acl-dscp-set}?
     |     |  +--rw fragment?           boolean
     |     |  +--rw first-fragment?     boolean
     |     |  +--rw icmp
     |     |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp-type
     |     |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |     |  +--rw protocol?           srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |     |  +--rw source-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  +--rw destination-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw source-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |     +--ro statistics
     |        +--ro last-clear?      srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro aggregate
     |        |  +--ro incomplete?            boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:future-0-0}?
     |        |  +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        |  +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        |  +--ro policer-stats
     |        |     +--ro in-conforming-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |     +--ro in-conforming-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |     +--ro in-exceeding-packets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |     +--ro in-exceeding-octets?      srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |     +--ro out-conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |     +--ro out-conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |     +--ro out-exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |     +--ro out-exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro per-interface {not srl_nokia-feat:future-0-0}?
     |           +--ro subinterface* [name]
     |              +--ro name                   string
     |              +--ro incomplete?            boolean

     +--rw subinterface* [id]

     |     +--ro session-state?                      bfd-session-state

module: srl_nokia-routing-policy
  +--rw routing-policy
     +--rw as-path-set* [name]
     |  +--rw name          srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw expression?   srl_nokia-pol-types:as-path-regexp
     +--rw prefix-set* [name]
     |  +--rw name      srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw prefix* [ip-prefix mask-length-range]
     |     +--rw ip-prefix            srl_nokia-comm:ip-prefix
     |     +--rw mask-length-range    string
     +--rw community-set* [name]
     |  +--rw name      srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw member*   union
     +--rw policy* [name]
        +--rw name              srl_nokia-comm:name
        +--rw default-action
        |  +--rw policy-result?   srl_nokia-pol-types:policy-result-type
        |  +--rw bgp
        |     +--rw as-path
        |     |  +--rw remove?    boolean
        |     |  +--rw replace*   srl_nokia-pol-types:as-number
        |     |  +--rw prepend
        |     |     +--rw as-number?   union
        |     |     +--rw repeat-n?    uint8
        |     +--rw communities
        |     |  +--rw add?       -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
        |     |  +--rw remove?    -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
        |     |  +--rw replace?   -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
        |     +--rw local-preference
        |     |  +--rw set?   uint32
        |     +--rw med {srl_nokia-feat:routing-policy-bgp-med}?
        |     |  +--rw set?   union
        |     +--rw origin
        |        +--rw set?   enumeration
        +--rw statement* [name]
           +--rw name      srl_nokia-comm:name
           +--rw match
           |  +--rw prefix-set?   -> /routing-policy/prefix-set/name
           |  +--rw bgp
           |  |  +--rw as-path-set?      -> /routing-policy/as-path-set/name
           |  |  +--rw as-path-length
           |  |  |  +--rw value?      uint8
           |  |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pol-types:comparison-operator-type
           |  |  |  +--rw unique?     boolean
           |  |  +--rw community-set?    -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
           |  |  +--rw evpn
           |  |     +--rw route-type*   uint8
           |  +--rw family*       srl_nokia-pol-types:bgp-family-type
           |  +--rw protocol?     identityref
           |  +--rw isis
           |  |  +--rw level?        uint8
           |  |  +--rw route-type?   enumeration
           |  +--rw ospf
           |     +--rw area-id?       srl_nokia-ospf-types:ospf-area-identifier
           |     +--rw route-type?    identityref
           |     +--rw instance-id?   uint32
           +--rw action
              +--rw policy-result?   srl_nokia-pol-types:policy-result-type
              +--rw bgp
                 +--rw as-path
                 |  +--rw remove?    boolean
                 |  +--rw replace*   srl_nokia-pol-types:as-number
                 |  +--rw prepend
                 |     +--rw as-number?   union
                 |     +--rw repeat-n?    uint8
                 +--rw communities
                 |  +--rw add?       -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
                 |  +--rw remove?    -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
                 |  +--rw replace?   -> /routing-policy/community-set/name
                 +--rw local-preference
                 |  +--rw set?   uint32
                 +--rw med {srl_nokia-feat:routing-policy-bgp-med}?
                 |  +--rw set?   union
                 +--rw origin
                    +--rw set?   enumeration

     +--rw srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:vxlan-tunnel

        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-discarded-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-octets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-packets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-discarded-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
        +--rw srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:statistics {srl_nokia-feat:vxlan-stats}?
           +--rw srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:admin-state?            srl_nokia-comm:admin-state
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-octets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-packets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-discarded-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-octets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-packets?            srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:last-clear?             srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
